<div class="sqs-html-content" data-sqsp-text-block-content>
  <h2 style="text-align:center;white-space:pre-wrap;">Spreading Awareness One Workshop at a Time</h2><p class="" style="white-space:pre-wrap;">An eczema awareness workshop led by a high school student turned into a powerful moment of storytelling, advocacy, and community care. Partnering with University Prep students, I shared my journey as a National Eczema Association Ambassador while we built care kits for people living with eczema, reminding us that confidence, kindness, and representation can start at any age.</p>
</div>

<div class="sqs-html-content" data-sqsp-text-block-content>
  <p class="sqsrte-large" style="white-space:pre-wrap;"><strong>I’m Darchelle D. Burnett, M.A.</strong><br>Creative inclusion consultant, artist, storyteller, and model. Many know me from my handmade small batch selection of scrunchies or from my eczema content and research. But I also help individuals and organizations translate lived experience into meaningful creative work  through workshops, visual storytelling, and intentional products.</p>

    <script defer="true" src="https://static1.squarespace.com/static/vta/5c5a519771c10ba3470d8101/scripts/site-bundle.ffb22c3e841b638295ea13d0eb1a9f48.js" type="text/javascript"></script>
    <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/jquery@3.6.0/dist/jquery.min.js"></script>
<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/readmore.js@2.0.4/readmore.js"></script>
<script>
  $(document).ready(function() {
    if (window.self!==window.top) {
      return;
    }
    
    $("[href='#read-more']").each(function(i, el) {
      // First calculate the initial space between the content and the readmore tag   
      const contentEl = $(el).closest(".html-block, .sqs-block-content, .summary-excerpt, .image-subtitle");
      const elBound = (el.getBoundingClientRect());
      const contentBound = (contentEl[0].getBoundingClientRect());
      contentEl.readmore({ 
        collapsedHeight: Math.floor(elBound.y - contentBound.y),
        speed: 500,
        embedCSS: true, 
        lessLink: '<a href="#" data-action="collapse-rmjs">Read less</a>'
      })
    });

    $(document).on("click", "[data-action='collapse-rmjs']", function() {
      const readmoreId = $(this).attr("aria-controls");	

      const contentEl = $(`#${readmoreId}`);
      if($(contentEl).closest('.sqs-block-image').length) {
        contentBound = $(contentEl).closest('.sqs-block-image')[0].getBoundingClientRect();
      } else {
        const contentBound = (contentEl[0].getBoundingClientRect());
      }
      window.scrollTo(0, windown.scrollY + contentBound.top);
    });
  });       
</script>

<style>
  /* Tweak readmore js to hide the placeholder link */
  [id*=rmjs] {
    transition: height 200ms;
    overflow: hidden;
  }
  [id*=rmjs] [href='#read-more'] {
    display: none;
  }
  body.sqs-edit-mode [href='#read-more'] {
    display: inline-block !important;	
  }

  [data-readmore-toggle] {
    /* color of read more */
